## 1. Schema Inicial (v1_initial_schema.sql)

```sql
-- src/database/schema/v1_initial_schema.sql

-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP V10 CORE DATABASE SCHEMA
-- Designed for performance and scalability
-- ============================================

-- Enable UUID extension for distributed systems
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- ============================================
-- CORE TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Users table with authentication and profile data
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(200),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    
    -- Authentication flags
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    is_admin BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Performance optimization: partial index for active users
    CONSTRAINT valid_email CHECK (email ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$')
);

-- Projects table - main entity for DIY projects
CREATE TABLE projects (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Project details
    title VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    difficulty_level VARCHAR(50) CHECK (difficulty_level IN ('beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced', 'expert')),
    
    -- Status tracking
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'draft' 
        CHECK (status IN ('draft', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'archived', 'published')),
    
    -- Metrics
    estimated_hours DECIMAL(5,2),
    actual_hours DECIMAL(5,2),
    cost_estimate DECIMAL(10,2),
    actual_cost DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Media
    cover_image_url TEXT,
    video_url TEXT,
    
    -- Timestamps with timezone for global users
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    published_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Full-text search vector
    search_vector TSVECTOR,
    
    -- Unique constraint per user
    UNIQUE(user_id, slug)
);

-- Tasks table - breakdown of project steps
CREATE TABLE tasks (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    parent_task_id UUID REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Task details
    title VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    step_number INTEGER,
    
    -- Status and tracking
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending' 
        CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'blocked', 'skipped')),
    priority VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'medium' 
        CHECK (priority IN ('low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical')),
    
    -- Time estimates
    estimated_minutes INTEGER,
    actual_minutes INTEGER,
    
    -- Dependencies and ordering
    depends_on_task_ids UUID[] DEFAULT '{}',
    sort_order INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Check constraint for positive time
    CONSTRAINT positive_time CHECK (estimated_minutes >= 0 AND actual_minutes >= 0)
);

-- Materials table - inventory for projects
CREATE TABLE materials (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    task_id UUID REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    
    -- Material details
    name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    category VARCHAR(100),
    quantity DECIMAL(10,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    unit VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Cost tracking
    unit_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_price DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (quantity * unit_price) STORED,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'needed' 
        CHECK (status IN ('needed', 'purchased', 'in_stock', 'used')),
    
    -- Vendor information
    vendor_name VARCHAR(200),
    vendor_url TEXT,
    sku VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    purchased_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
);

-- ============================================
-- AI/LLM INTERACTION TABLES
-- ============================================

-- LLM Interactions table - track all AI interactions
CREATE TABLE llm_interactions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    project_id UUID REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    task_id UUID REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    
    -- LLM Provider details
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL 
        CHECK (provider IN ('openai', 'anthropic', 'google', 'azure', 'local')),
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    api_endpoint VARCHAR(500),
    
    -- Request/Response tracking
    prompt TEXT NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    response TEXT,
    response_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (prompt_tokens + COALESCE(response_tokens, 0)) STORED,
    
    -- Cost tracking (in USD)
    cost_per_token DECIMAL(12,10),
    total_cost DECIMAL(12,6) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (total_tokens * cost_per_token) STORED,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Context and purpose
    interaction_type VARCHAR(50) 
        CHECK (interaction_type IN ('project_planning', 'task_breakdown', 'material_suggestions', 
               'troubleshooting', 'creative_ideas', 'code_generation', 'documentation')),
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Index-friendly columns for common queries
    date_created DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::DATE) STORED
);

-- AI Model Performance tracking
CREATE TABLE ai_model_performance (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    avg_tokens_per_second DECIMAL(10,2),
    success_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    avg_cost_per_request DECIMAL(12,6),
    
    -- Usage statistics
    total_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost DECIMAL(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Time window
    time_period VARCHAR(20) 
        CHECK (time_period IN ('hourly', 'daily', 'weekly', 'monthly')),
    period_start TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    period_end TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Metadata
    calculated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(model_name, provider, time_period, period_start)
);

-- ============================================
-- AUDIT AND ANALYTICS TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Audit log for all significant actions
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    
    -- Actor information
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    user_ip INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    -- Action details
    action_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    resource_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    resource_id UUID,
    
    -- Changes (stored as JSON for flexibility)
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Partition key for time-based partitioning
    log_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::DATE) STORED
) PARTITION BY RANGE (log_date);

-- User analytics for behavior tracking
CREATE TABLE user_analytics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Engagement metrics
    sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    session_duration_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    page_views INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Project metrics
    projects_created INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    projects_completed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    tasks_completed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- AI usage
    llm_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    llm_tokens_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    llm_cost DECIMAL(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    avg_task_completion_time INTEGER,
    
    -- Metadata
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(user_id, date)
);

-- ============================================
-- RELATIONSHIP TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Project collaborators (many-to-many)
CREATE TABLE project_collaborators (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Role and permissions
    role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'viewer' 
        CHECK (role IN ('viewer', 'editor', 'admin', 'owner')),
    permissions JSONB DEFAULT '{"read": true, "write": false, "delete": false}',
    
    -- Invitation status
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending' 
        CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'accepted', 'rejected', 'revoked')),
    
    -- Metadata
    invited_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    joined_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(project_id, user_id)
);

-- Project tags (many-to-many)
CREATE TABLE project_tags (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    tag_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(project_id, tag_name)
);

-- Task dependencies (many-to-many)
CREATE TABLE task_dependencies (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    task_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    depends_on_task_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    dependency_type VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'finish_to_start' 
        CHECK (dependency_type IN ('finish_to_start', 'start_to_start', 'finish_to_finish', 'start_to_finish')),
    
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(task_id, depends_on_task_id),
    CONSTRAINT no_self_dependency CHECK (task_id != depends_on_task_id)
);

-- ============================================
-- SYSTEM TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Migration tracking
CREATE TABLE schema_migrations (
    version VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    applied_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    checksum VARCHAR(64)
);

-- System configuration
CREATE TABLE system_config (
    key VARCHAR(200) PRIMARY KEY,
    value JSONB NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- Rate limiting and quotas
CREATE TABLE rate_limits (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    endpoint VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Rate limiting counters
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    token_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Time window
    window_start TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    window_end TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Limits
    max_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 1000,
    max_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 1000000,
    
    -- Metadata
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    UNIQUE(user_id, endpoint, window_start)
);

-- ============================================
-- FUNCTIONS AND TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Function to update updated_at timestamp
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Function to generate project slug
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION generate_project_slug(title VARCHAR, user_id UUID)
RETURNS VARCHAR AS $$
DECLARE
    base_slug VARCHAR;
    final_slug VARCHAR;
    counter INTEGER := 1;
BEGIN
    -- Convert title to slug
    base_slug := lower(regexp_replace(title, '[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', '-', 'g'));
    base_slug := regexp_replace(base_slug, '^-|-$', '', 'g');
    
    final_slug := base_slug;
    
    -- Check for existing slugs for this user
    WHILE EXISTS (
        SELECT 1 FROM projects 
        WHERE projects.user_id = $2 
        AND projects.slug = final_slug
    ) LOOP
        final_slug := base_slug || '-' || counter;
        counter := counter + 1;
    END LOOP;
    
    RETURN final_slug;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Function to update search vector for projects
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_project_search_vector()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.search_vector := 
        setweight(to_tsvector('english', COALESCE(NEW.title, '')), 'A') ||
        setweight(to_tsvector('english', COALESCE(NEW.description, '')), 'B') ||
        setweight(to_tsvector('english', COALESCE(NEW.category, '')), 'C');
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- ============================================
-- TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Update timestamps for all tables
CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON users 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_projects_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON projects 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_tasks_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON tasks 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_materials_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON materials 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Update project search vector
CREATE TRIGGER update_project_search_vector 
    BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE ON projects 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_project_search_vector();

-- Auto-generate slug on project insert
CREATE TRIGGER generate_project_slug_trigger
    BEFORE INSERT ON projects
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE FUNCTION generate_project_slug(NEW.title, NEW.user_id);
```

## 2. Estratégia de Indexação (v2_indexes_performance.sql)

```sql
-- src/database/schema/v2_indexes_performance.sql

-- ============================================
-- PERFORMANCE INDEXES FOR DIYAPP V10
-- Optimized for common query patterns
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- USERS TABLE INDEXES
-- ============================================

-- Primary lookup by email (login)
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);

-- Lookup by username
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);

-- Active users (common filter)
CREATE INDEX idx_users_active ON users(is_active) WHERE is_active = TRUE;

-- Admin users (for admin operations)
CREATE INDEX idx_users_admin ON users(is_admin) WHERE is_admin = TRUE;

-- Created date for user growth analytics
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at DESC);

-- Composite index for user search
CREATE INDEX idx_users_search ON users(email, username, full_name);

-- ============================================
-- PROJECTS TABLE INDEXES
-- ============================================

-- Primary lookup by user (user's projects)
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_user

## ADR 001: Frontend Framework Decision

**ADR-001: Seleção do Framework Frontend - React com TypeScript e Vite**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Frontend Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos de um framework frontend que ofereça:
1. Alta produtividade para desenvolvimento de interfaces complexas
2. Forte tipagem para prevenir erros em runtime
3. Excelente experiência de desenvolvimento (hot reload, fast builds)
4. Ecossistema maduro com ampla adoção na indústria
5. Compatibilidade com componentes de IA e dashboards em tempo real

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar **React 18+ com TypeScript** como framework principal, utilizando **Vite** como build tool.

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: React + TypeScript + Vite**
- Prós: 
  - Ecossistema maduro e vasta comunidade
  - Forte tipagem com TypeScript
  - Vite oferece build times extremamente rápidos
  - Hooks API moderna e eficiente
  - Amplo suporte a bibliotecas de UI
- Contras:
  - Necessidade de escolher bibliotecas adicionais (roteamento, estado)
  - Curva de aprendizado para padrões avançados

**Opção B: Next.js 14 (App Router)**
- Prós:
  - Roteamento e SSR built-in
  - Otimizações automáticas de performance
  - Suporte a Server Components
- Contras:
  - Menor flexibilidade em configuração
  - Overhead para aplicações que não precisam de SSR
  - Lock-in mais forte com a plataforma

**Opção C: Vue 3 + Composition API**
- Prós:
  - Sintaxe mais simples para alguns casos
  - Performance excelente
  - Documentação excelente
- Contras:
  - Ecossistema menor que React
  - Menor adoção em projetos enterprise

**Opção escolhida: A** 
**Justificativa:** React oferece o melhor equilíbrio entre flexibilidade, ecossistema e manutenibilidade. Vite resolve os problemas de build time do Webpack. TypeScript é essencial para qualidade de código em squads autônomas.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Desenvolvimento rápido com hot reload
- Código mais seguro com TypeScript
- Fácil contratação de desenvolvedores
- Compatibilidade com bibliotecas de visualização de dados

**Negativas:**
- Necessidade de configurar roteamento (React Router)
- Gerenciamento de estado precisa de biblioteca adicional (Zustand/Redux Toolkit)

**Riscos:**
- Configuração inicial mais complexa (mitigado por templates e scripts)
- Bundle size maior se não controlado (mitigado por code splitting)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-07-15 (6 meses)

---

## ADR 002: Backend Architecture

**ADR-002: Arquitetura Backend - Node.js com Express e Arquitetura em Camadas**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Backend Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
O backend precisa:
1. Escalar horizontalmente
2. Manter baixa latência para operações de IA
3. Ser fácil de testar e manter
4. Suportar múltiplos protocolos (HTTP, WebSocket, gRPC)
5. Ter observabilidade built-in

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar **Node.js + Express** com arquitetura em camadas (Controller → Service → Repository).

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: Node.js + Express (Arquitetura em Camadas)**
- Prós:
  - Performance excelente para I/O
  - JavaScript/TypeScript em full-stack
  - Middleware ecosystem maduro
  - Fácil deploy e scaling
- Contras:
  - Single-threaded (mitigado por clustering)
  - Callback hell (mitigado por async/await)

**Opção B: NestJS**
- Prós:
  - Arquitetura opinada e bem definida
  - Injeção de dependências built-in
  - Muitos módulos prontos
- Contras:
  - Curva de aprendizado mais íngreme
  - Overhead de abstrações
  - Menor flexibilidade

**Opção C: Go (Gin/Fiber)**
- Prós:
  - Performance excepcional
  - Concorrência nativa
  - Binário standalone
- Contras:
  - Nova linguagem para a squad
  - Ecossistema menor para IA
  - Dupla stack de linguagens

**Opção escolhida: A**
**Justificativa:** Node.js oferece a melhor produtividade para squads full-stack. A arquitetura em camadas garante separação de concerns e testabilidade.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Code sharing entre frontend e backend
- Vasta biblioteca de pacotes npm
- Fácil integração com serviços de IA
- Boa performance para APIs REST/WebSocket

**Negativas:**
- Necessidade de patterns para evitar callback hell
- Gerenciamento manual de injeção de dependências

**Riscos:**
- Memory leaks em aplicações de longa duração (mitigado por monitoring)
- Callback hell (mitigado por async/await e padrões)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-07-15

---

## ADR 003: Database ORM

**ADR-003: ORM e Estratégia de Banco de Dados**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Infra Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos de:
1. Suporte a PostgreSQL (transacional) e Redis (cache/sessão)
2. Migrações versionadas e reversíveis
3. Type safety nas queries
4. Performance em queries complexas
5. Suporte a transações

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar **Prisma** como ORM principal e **ioredis** para Redis.

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: Prisma + ioredis**
- Prós:
  - Type safety excelente
  - Migrações automáticas e seguras
  - Query builder intuitivo
  - Performance boa com connection pooling
  - Client gerado automaticamente
- Contras:
  - Learning curve para relações complexas
  - Bundle size maior

**Opção B: TypeORM + redis**
- Prós:
  - Padrão Active Record familiar
  - Suporte a múltiplos bancos
  - Decorators para definição de modelos
- Contras:
  - Type safety inferior ao Prisma
  - Performance queries complexas
  - Documentação menos consistente

**Opção C: Drizzle + upstash/redis**
- Prós:
  - Type safety excelente
  - Performance superior
  - SQL-like syntax
- Contras:
  - Ecossistema mais novo
  - Menor adoção em produção

**Opção escolhida: A**
**Justificativa:** Prisma oferece a melhor experiência de desenvolvimento com type safety end-to-end. As migrações automáticas são cruciais para deploy contínuo.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Queries type-safe
- Migrações versionadas no git
- Auto-complete no VS Code
- Fácil switching entre dev/prod

**Negativas:**
- Necessidade de gerar client após mudanças no schema
- Learning curve para otimizações avançadas

**Riscos:**
- Performance em queries muito complexas (mitigado por raw queries quando necessário)
- Vendor lock-in leve (mitigado por abstração do repositório)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15 (3 meses)

---

## ADR 004: Caching Strategy

**ADR-004: Estratégia de Cache em Camadas**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Infra Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
O sistema precisa:
1. Cache em múltiplos níveis (browser, CDN, servidor)
2. Invalidação eficiente de cache
3. Cache para dados de IA (embeddings, modelos)
4. Estratégia para dados frequentemente acessados

**DECISÃO:**
Implementar cache em 3 camadas:
1. **Browser Cache:** Cache-Control headers para assets estáticos
2. **CDN Cache:** Cloudflare para conteúdo dinâmico
3. **Server Cache:** Redis para dados de aplicação

**ESTRATÉGIA DETALHADA:**

```typescript
// Estratégia de cache por tipo de dado
export enum CacheStrategy {
  NO_CACHE = 'no-cache',           // Dados sempre frescos
  SHORT_TTL = 'short-ttl',         // 5 minutos (dados semi-dinâmicos)
  LONG_TTL = 'long-ttl',           // 1 hora (dados estáticos)
  INFINITE = 'infinite',           // Até invalidação manual
  STALE_WHILE_REVALIDATE = 'swr',  // Serve stale, atualiza em background
}

// Padrão de chaves de cache
// app:version:resource:id:query
// Ex: diyapp:v10:user:123:profile
```

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: Cache em Camadas (escolhida)**
- Prós:
  - Reduz carga no banco de dados
  - Melhora latência para usuários
  - Escalabilidade horizontal
  - Flexibilidade por tipo de dado
- Contras:
  - Complexidade de invalidação
  - Consistency challenges

**Opção B: Cache-Aside Pattern**
- Prós:
  - Simples de implementar
  - Fail-safe (se cache falha, vai no banco)
- Contras:
  - Cache stampede risk
  - Data staleness

**Opção C: Write-Through Cache**
- Prós:
  - Data sempre consistente
  - Bom para write-heavy workloads
- Contras:
  - Latência maior em writes
  - Overhead em todas as escritas

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Latência reduzida em 60-80%
- Carga no banco reduzida significativamente
- Melhor experiência do usuário

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade adicional
- Necessidade de monitorar hit/miss rates
- Memory overhead

**Riscos:**
- Cache inconsistency (mitigado por TTLs adequados e invalidação)
- Memory pressure no Redis (mitigado por eviction policies)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-03-15 (2 meses)

---

## ADR 005: Error Handling & Logging

**ADR-005: Estratégia Unificada de Tratamento de Erros e Logging**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Security Specialist

**CONTEXTO:**
Sistema precisa de:
1. Logs estruturados para debugging
2. Tratamento consistente de erros
3. Alertas automáticos para erros críticos
4. Rastreamento de requests end-to-end
5. Compliance com GDPR/security

**DECISÃO:**
Implementar:
1. **Winston** para logging estruturado
2. **Error boundaries** no frontend
3. **Global error handler** no backend
4. **Request ID** para tracing
5. **Sentry** para error tracking em produção

**PADRÕES DE LOG:**

```typescript
// Níveis de log
export enum LogLevel {
  ERROR = 'error',     // Erros que precisam atenção imediata
  WARN = 'warn',       // Situações anômalas mas não críticas
  INFO = 'info',       // Informações de operação normal
  DEBUG = 'debug',     // Informações detalhadas para debugging
  HTTP = 'http',       // Requests HTTP
}

// Estrutura do log
interface LogEntry {
  timestamp: string;
  level: LogLevel;
  message: string;
  requestId?: string;
  userId?: string;
  sessionId?: string;
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
  stack?: string; // apenas para errors
}
```

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Debugging mais fácil com logs estruturados
- Monitoring proativo de erros
- Tracing de requests completo
- Compliance com auditorias

**Negativas:**
- Volume maior de dados de log
- Performance overhead mínimo
- Complexidade de configuração

**Riscos:**
- Log de dados sensíveis (mitigado por sanitização)
- Performance impact (mitigado por log levels apropriados)

**REVISÃO:** 2024-02-15 (1 mês)

---

## Engineering Standards Document

```markdown
# DIYAPP V10 - Engineering Standards

## 1. Code Style & Formatting

### TypeScript/JavaScript
- Use TypeScript strict mode
- 2 spaces indentation
- Single quotes for strings
- Semicolons required
- Max line length: 100 characters
- Use `interface` over `type` for object definitions

### React Components
- Functional components only (no class components)
- Use named exports over default exports
- One component per file
- Use TypeScript for props
- Destructure props in function signature

### Naming Conventions
- PascalCase: Components, Interfaces, Types, Classes
- camelCase: variables, functions, methods
- UPPER_SNAKE_CASE: constants
- kebab-case: files, folders, URLs

## 2. Git & Version Control

### Branch Strategy
- `main`: Production ready code
- `develop`: Integration branch
- `feature/*`: New features
- `fix/*`: Bug fixes
- `hotfix/*`: Critical production fixes

### Commit Messages (Conventional Commits)
```
<type>(<scope>): <description>

[optional body]

[optional footer]
```

Types:
- `feat`: New feature
- `fix`: Bug fix
- `docs`: Documentation
- `style`: Formatting
- `refactor`: Code restructuring
- `test`: Adding tests
- `chore`: Maintenance

### Pull Requests
- One PR per feature/fix
- Max 400 lines changed
- Description must include:
  - What changed
  - Why it changed
  - Testing performed
  - Screenshots (UI changes)
- All checks must pass
- Requires 1 approval minimum

## 3. Testing Strategy

### Test Pyramid
- Unit Tests: 70% coverage
- Integration Tests: 20% coverage
- E2E Tests: 10% coverage

### Minimum Coverage
- Overall: 80%
- Critical paths: 90%
- New code: 90%

### Test Structure
```typescript
describe('Component/Service Name', () => {
  describe('methodName', () => {
    it('should do something when condition', () => {
      // Arrange
      // Act
      // Assert
    });
    
    it('should handle error case', () => {
      // Test error scenarios
    });
  });
});
```

## 4. API Design

### REST Guidelines
- Use nouns for resources (not verbs)
- Plural resource names
- Version in URL: `/api/v1/resource`
- Filter, sort, paginate via query params
- Consistent error responses

### Response Format
```typescript
{
  "success": boolean,
  "data": any,          // null on error
  "error": {            // null on success
    "code": string,
    "message": string,
    "details": any
  },
  "meta": {             // pagination, etc
    "page": number,
    "total": number,
    "timestamp": string
  }
}
```

### Error Codes
- 400: Bad Request (validation errors)
- 401: Unauthorized
- 403: Forbidden
- 404: Not Found
- 429: Too Many Requests
- 500: Internal Server Error

## 5. Security Standards

###

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Configuração de Ambiente

Vou configurar o ambiente de desenvolvimento V10 com Vite + React, seguindo os padrões de qualidade e estrutura profissional exigidos.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── public/
├── src/
│   ├── components/
│   ├── hooks/
│   ├── utils/

│   └── main.tsx

## 11. src/App.tsx

```typescript
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { Suspense, lazy } from 'react'
import Layout from '@/components/Layout'
import LoadingSpinner from '@/components/LoadingSpinner'

// Lazy loading para code splitting
const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('@/pages/Dashboard'))
const Projects = lazy(() => import('@/pages/Projects'))
const Automation = lazy(() => import('@/pages/Automation'))
const Settings = lazy(() => import('@/pages/Settings'))

function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Layout>
        <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/projects" element={<Projects />} />
            <Route path="/automation" element={<Automation />} />
            <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
          </Routes>
        </Suspense>
      </Layout>
    </Router>
  )
}

export default App
```

```typescript
// src/core/repositories/base.repository.ts
import { PrismaClient, Prisma } from '@prisma/client';

export abstract class BaseRepository<T> {
  protected prisma: PrismaClient;
  protected model: keyof PrismaClient;

  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient, model: keyof PrismaClient) {
    this.prisma = prisma;
    this.model = model;
  }

  protected getModel(): any {
    return (this.prisma as any)[this.model as string];
  }

  async create(data: any): Promise<T> {
    try {
      const result = await this.getModel().create({ data });
      return result as T;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  async findById(id: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      const result = await this.getModel().findUnique({
        where: { id }
      });
      return result as T | null;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  async findMany(filter: any, options?: {
    skip?: number;
    take?: number;
    orderBy?: any;
  }): Promise<T[]> {
    try {
      const result = await this.getModel().findMany({
        where: filter,
        skip: options?.skip,
        take: options?.take,
        orderBy: options?.orderBy
      });
      return result as T[];
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  async update(id: string, data: any): Promise<T> {
    try {
      const result = await this.getModel().update({
        where: { id },
        data
      });
      return result as T;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  async delete(id: string): Promise<T> {
    try {
      const result = await this.getModel().delete({
        where: { id }
      });
      return result as T;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  async count(filter: any): Promise<number> {
    try {
      return await this.getModel().count({ where: filter });
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleDatabaseError(error);
    }
  }

  protected handleDatabaseError(error: any): never {
    // Log structured error
    console.error(JSON.stringify({
      level: 'error',
      correlation_id: this.generateCorrelationId(),
      message: 'Database operation failed',
      error: error.message,
      stack: error.stack,
      model: this.model
    }));

    // Map Prisma errors to appropriate HTTP status codes
    if (error instanceof Prisma.PrismaClientKnownRequestError) {
      switch (error.code) {
        case 'P2002':
          throw new Error('Unique constraint violation');
        case 'P2025':
          throw new Error('Record not found');
        case 'P2003':
          throw new Error('Foreign key constraint failed');
        default:
          throw new Error('Database error occurred');
      }
    }

    throw new Error('Internal server error');
  }

  private generateCorrelationId(): string {
    return `corr_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/core/repositories/agent.repository.ts
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { BaseRepository } from './base.repository';
import { Agent, AgentCapability, AgentMetrics } from '../models';

export class AgentRepository extends BaseRepository<Agent> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'agent');
  }

  async findByRole(role: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
    return this.findMany({ role });
  }

  async findActiveAgents(): Promise<Agent[]> {
    return this.findMany({ status: 'active' });
  }

  async updateCapabilities(agentId: string, capabilities: string[]): Promise<Agent> {
    return this.update(agentId, {
      capabilities,
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async deactivateAgent(agentId: string): Promise<Agent> {
    return this.update(agentId, {
      status: 'inactive',
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }
}

export class AgentCapabilityRepository extends BaseRepository<AgentCapability> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'agentCapability');
  }

  async updateProficiency(agentId: string, capability: string, proficiency: number): Promise<AgentCapability> {
    const existing = await this.findMany({ agentId, capability });
    
    if (existing.length > 0) {
      return this.update(existing[0].id, {
        proficiency,
        lastUsed: new Date()
      });
    } else {
      return this.create({
        agentId,
        capability,
        proficiency,
        lastUsed: new Date()
      });
    }
  }

  async getAgentCapabilities(agentId: string): Promise<AgentCapability[]> {
    return this.findMany({ agentId });
  }
}

export class AgentMetricsRepository extends BaseRepository<AgentMetrics> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'agentMetrics');
  }

  async recordExecution(
    agentId: string,
    success: boolean,
    executionTime: number
  ): Promise<AgentMetrics> {
    const existing = await this.findById(agentId);
    
    const totalExecutions = (existing?.totalExecutions || 0) + 1;
    const successCount = (existing?.successRate || 0) * (totalExecutions - 1) / 100;
    const newSuccessRate = ((successCount + (success ? 1 : 0)) / totalExecutions) * 100;
    
    const avgExecutionTime = existing
      ? (existing.avgExecutionTime * (totalExecutions - 1) + executionTime) / totalExecutions
      : executionTime;

    const data = {
      agentId,
      totalExecutions,
      successRate: newSuccessRate,
      avgExecutionTime,
      lastExecution: new Date()
    };

    if (existing) {
      return this.update(agentId, data);
    } else {
      return this.create(data);
    }
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/core/repositories/project.repository.ts
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { BaseRepository } from './base.repository';
import { Project, ProjectMember, ProjectSettings } from '../models';

export class ProjectRepository extends BaseRepository<Project> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'project');
  }

  async findByOwner(ownerId: string): Promise<Project[]> {
    return this.findMany({ ownerId });
  }

  async findByTeam(teamId: string): Promise<Project[]> {
    return this.findMany({ teamId });
  }

  async archiveProject(projectId: string): Promise<Project> {
    return this.update(projectId, {
      status: 'archived',
      updatedAt: new Date(),
      deletedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async updateSettings(projectId: string, settings: Partial<ProjectSettings>): Promise<Project> {
    const project = await this.findById(projectId);
    if (!project) {
      throw new Error('Project not found');
    }

    const updatedSettings = {
      ...project.settings,
      ...settings
    };

    return this.update(projectId, {
      settings: updatedSettings,
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }
}

export class ProjectMemberRepository extends BaseRepository<ProjectMember> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'projectMember');
  }

  async addMember(projectId: string, userId: string, role: ProjectMember['role']): Promise<ProjectMember> {
    return this.create({
      projectId,
      userId,
      role,
      joinedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async updateMemberRole(projectId: string, userId: string, role: ProjectMember['role']): Promise<ProjectMember> {
    const member = await this.findMany({ projectId, userId });
    if (member.length === 0) {
      throw new Error('Member not found');
    }

    return this.update(member[0].id, { role });
  }

  async getProjectMembers(projectId: string): Promise<ProjectMember[]> {
    return this.findMany({ projectId });
  }

  async removeMember(projectId: string, userId: string): Promise<void> {
    const member = await this.findMany({ projectId, userId });
    if (member.length > 0) {
      await this.delete(member[0].id);
    }
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/core/repositories/conversation.repository.ts
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { BaseRepository } from './base.repository';
import { Conversation, Message, ConversationContext } from '../models';

export class ConversationRepository extends BaseRepository<Conversation> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'conversation');
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Conversation[]> {
    return this.findMany({ projectId });
  }

  async updateContext(conversationId: string, context: Partial<ConversationContext>): Promise<Conversation> {
    const conversation = await this.findById(conversationId);
    if (!conversation) {
      throw new Error('Conversation not found');
    }

    const updatedContext = {
      ...conversation.context,
      ...context
    };

    return this.update(conversationId, {
      context: updatedContext,
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async archiveConversation(conversationId: string): Promise<Conversation> {
    return this.update(conversationId, {
      status: 'archived',
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }
}

export class MessageRepository extends BaseRepository<Message> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'message');
  }

  async findByConversation(conversationId: string, options?: {
    skip?: number;
    take?: number;
    orderBy?: 'asc' | 'desc';
  }): Promise<Message[]> {
    return this.findMany(
      { conversationId },
      {
        skip: options?.skip,
        take: options?.take,
        orderBy: { createdAt: options?.orderBy || 'asc' }
      }
    );
  }

  async addMessage(message: Omit<Message, 'id' | 'createdAt'>): Promise<Message> {
    return this.create({
      ...message,
      createdAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async getConversationThread(parentMessageId: string): Promise<Message[]> {
    // This would need a recursive query or a different approach
    // For now, return messages with this parent
    return this.findMany({ parentMessageId });
  }

  async updateMessageTokens(messageId: string, tokens: number): Promise<Message> {
    return this.update(messageId, { tokens });
  }
}

// src/core/repositories/task.repository.ts
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { BaseRepository } from './base.repository';
import { Task, TaskArtifact } from '../models';

export class TaskRepository extends BaseRepository<Task> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'task');
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Task[]> {
    return this.findMany({ projectId });
  }

  async findByStatus(status: Task['status']): Promise<Task[]> {
    return this.findMany({ status });
  }

  async assignTask(taskId: string, agentId: string): Promise<Task> {
    return this.update(taskId, {
      assignedAgentId: agentId,
      status: 'in_progress',
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async completeTask(taskId: string, actualEffort: number): Promise<Task> {
    return this.update(taskId, {
      status: 'completed',
      actualEffort,
      completedAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async getPendingTasks(agentId?: string): Promise<Task[]> {
    const filter: any = { status: 'pending' };
    if (agentId) {
      filter.assignedAgentId = agentId;
    }
    
    return this.findMany(filter, {
      orderBy: { priority: 'desc' }
    });
  }

  async addDependency(taskId: string, dependencyId: string): Promise<Task> {
    const task = await this.findById(taskId);
    if (!task) {
      throw new Error('Task not found');
    }

    const dependencies = [...task.dependencies, dependencyId];
    return this.update(taskId, {
      dependencies,
      updatedAt: new Date()
    });
  }
}

export class TaskArtifactRepository extends BaseRepository<TaskArtifact> {
  constructor(prisma: PrismaClient) {
    super(prisma, 'taskArtifact');
  }

  async findByTask(taskId: string): Promise<TaskArtifact[]> {
    return this.findMany({ taskId });
  }

  async findByType(taskId: string, type: TaskArtifact['type']): Promise<TaskArtifact[]> {
    return this.findMany({ taskId, type });
  }

  async storeArtifact(artifact: Omit<TaskArtifact, 'id' | 'createdAt'>): Promise<TaskArtifact> {
    return this.create({
      ...artifact,
      createdAt: new Date()
    });
  }

  async getArtifactContent(artifactId: string): Promise<string | undefined> {
    const artifact = await this.findById(artifactId

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Database Schema Design

## 1. Estrutura de Diretórios do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── database/
│   ├── schema/
│   │   ├── v1_initial_schema.sql
│   │   ├── v2_indexes_optimization.sql
│   │   └── v3_partitioning_strategy.sql
│   ├── migrations/
│   │   ├── 001_initial_schema.sql
│   │   ├── 002_create_indexes.sql
│   │   └── 003_partition_tables.sql
│   ├── scripts/
│   │   ├── setup_database.sh
│   │   ├── run_migrations.py
│   │   └── performance_benchmark.sql
│   └── config/
│       └── database_config.yaml
├── src/
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── user.py
│   │   ├── content.py
│   │   ├── interaction.py

│       └── connection.py
└── README.md

## 2. Schema Inicial Otimizado (PostgreSQL 14+)

**database/schema/v1_initial_schema.sql**

```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP V10 CORE - INITIAL SCHEMA
-- Optimized for performance and scalability
-- ============================================

-- Enable essential extensions
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pg_stat_statements";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "btree_gin";

-- ============================================
-- CORE TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Users table with partitioning-ready structure
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    username VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    display_name VARCHAR(150),
    hashed_password VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    account_status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active' 
        CHECK (account_status IN ('active', 'suspended', 'deactivated', 'pending')),
    
    -- Profile information
    avatar_url TEXT,
    bio TEXT,
    location VARCHAR(100),
    website_url TEXT,
    
    -- Preferences (JSONB for flexibility)
    preferences JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    
    -- Security
    two_factor_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    last_password_change TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Timestamps with precision
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Audit fields
    created_by_ip INET,
    last_login_ip INET,
    
    -- Soft delete
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- Content table with versioning support
CREATE TABLE content (
    content_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Content metadata
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(600) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    content_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL 
        CHECK (content_type IN ('article', 'tutorial', 'project', 'question', 'answer', 'comment')),
    
    -- Content hierarchy
    parent_content_id UUID REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    root_content_id UUID REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Content body (consider TEXT for large content, JSONB for structured)
    content_body TEXT,
    content_json JSONB,
    excerpt TEXT,
    
    -- Metadata
    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT '{}',
    category VARCHAR(100),
    language VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en',
    
    -- Status and visibility
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'draft' 
        CHECK (status IN ('draft', 'published', 'archived', 'deleted', 'pending_review')),
    visibility VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'public' 
        CHECK (visibility IN ('public', 'private', 'unlisted', 'followers_only')),
    
    -- Engagement metrics (denormalized for performance)
    view_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    like_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    comment_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    share_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    bookmark_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Quality signals
    featured BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    featured_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    featured_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    
    -- Versioning
    version INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    previous_version_id UUID,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    published_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- SEO/Discovery
    meta_title VARCHAR(600),
    meta_description TEXT,
    canonical_url TEXT,
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED,
    published_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (published_at::date) STORED
);

-- Interactions table (likes, bookmarks, etc.)
CREATE TABLE interactions (
    interaction_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    content_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    interaction_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL 
        CHECK (interaction_type IN ('like', 'bookmark', 'share', 'report', 'vote_up', 'vote_down')),
    
    -- Metadata
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Unique constraint to prevent duplicate interactions
    UNIQUE(user_id, content_id, interaction_type),
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- Comments table with threading support
CREATE TABLE comments (
    comment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    content_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    parent_comment_id UUID REFERENCES comments(comment_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Comment content
    comment_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    comment_html TEXT,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'published' 
        CHECK (status IN ('published', 'deleted', 'hidden', 'pending')),
    
    -- Moderation
    moderated BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    moderated_by UUID REFERENCES users(user_id),
    moderation_reason TEXT,
    
    -- Engagement
    like_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    reply_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- Follow relationships
CREATE TABLE follows (
    follower_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    following_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Relationship type
    relationship_type VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'follow' 
        CHECK (relationship_type IN ('follow', 'block', 'mute')),
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Primary key
    PRIMARY KEY (follower_id, following_id, relationship_type),
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- ============================================
-- ANALYTICS TABLES (Time-series optimized)
-- ============================================

-- Page views and engagement analytics
CREATE TABLE page_views (
    view_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    session_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    content_id UUID REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    
    -- Page information
    page_url TEXT NOT NULL,
    page_title VARCHAR(500),
    referrer_url TEXT,
    referrer_domain VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Device and browser info
    user_agent TEXT,
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    browser_name VARCHAR(100),
    browser_version VARCHAR(50),
    os_name VARCHAR(100),
    os_version VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Location
    ip_address INET,
    country_code CHAR(2),
    region VARCHAR(100),
    city VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Engagement metrics
    time_on_page INTEGER, -- in seconds
    scroll_depth INTEGER, -- percentage 0-100
    is_bounce BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- For time-series partitioning
    view_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED,
    view_hour INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (EXTRACT(HOUR FROM created_at)) STORED
);

-- Search analytics
CREATE TABLE search_queries (
    query_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Query data
    query_text TEXT NOT NULL,
    query_filters JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    
    -- Results
    result_count INTEGER,
    clicked_result_id UUID,
    clicked_position INTEGER,
    
    -- Performance
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- For partitioning
    query_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- ============================================
-- SYSTEM TABLES
-- ============================================

-- API rate limiting
CREATE TABLE api_rate_limits (
    rate_limit_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    api_key VARCHAR(100),
    endpoint VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Rate limiting
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    limit_value INTEGER NOT NULL,
    window_size INTEGER NOT NULL, -- in seconds
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Index for cleanup
    INDEX idx_api_rate_limits_expires (expires_at)
);

-- Audit log for compliance
CREATE TABLE audit_log (
    audit_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    
    -- Action details
    action_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    resource_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    resource_id UUID,
    
    -- Changes (JSONB for flexibility)
    old_values JSONB,
    new_values JSONB,
    
    -- Context
    ip_address INET,
    user_agent TEXT,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- For partitioning
    audit_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- ============================================
-- LOOKUP TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Categories (normalized for consistency)
CREATE TABLE categories (
    category_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    slug VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    description TEXT,
    parent_category_id UUID REFERENCES categories(category_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Display
    display_order INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    icon_url TEXT,
    color_hex CHAR(7),
    
    -- Stats (denormalized)
    content_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tags (normalized)
CREATE TABLE tags (
    tag_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    slug VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    description TEXT,
    
    -- Stats
    usage_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Content-tags relationship (many-to-many)
CREATE TABLE content_tags (
    content_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES content(content_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    tag_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tags(tag_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    PRIMARY KEY (content_id, tag_id)
);

-- ============================================
-- NOTIFICATION SYSTEM
-- ============================================

CREATE TABLE notifications (
    notification_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Notification details
    notification_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    message TEXT NOT NULL,
    
    -- Action
    action_url TEXT,
    action_label VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Metadata
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
    
    -- Status
    is_read BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_archived BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Priority
    priority VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'normal' 
        CHECK (priority IN ('low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent')),
    
    -- Timestamps
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    read_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- For partitioning
    created_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (created_at::date) STORED
);

-- ============================================
-- FUNCTIONS AND TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Function to update updated_at timestamp
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Triggers for updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON users 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_content_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON content 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_comments_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON comments 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_categories_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON categories 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_tags_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON tags 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Function to update comment counts
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_comment_count()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    IF TG_OP = 'INSERT' AND NEW.status = 'published' THEN
        UPDATE content 
        SET comment_count = comment_count + 1 
        WHERE content_id = NEW.content_id;
    ELSIF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
        IF OLD.status != 'published' AND NEW.status = 'published' THEN
            UPDATE content 
            SET comment_count = comment_count + 1 
            WHERE content_id = NEW.content_id;
        ELSIF OLD.status = 'published' AND NEW.status != 'published' THEN
            UPDATE content 
            SET comment_count = comment_count - 1 
            WHERE content_id = NEW.content_id;
        END IF;
    ELSIF TG_OP = 'DELETE' AND OLD.status = 'published' THEN
        UPDATE content 
        SET comment_count = comment_count - 1 
        WHERE content_id = OLD.content_id;
    END IF;
    RETURN NULL;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Trigger for comment counts
CREATE TRIGGER update_comment_counts
    AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE OR DELETE ON comments
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_comment_count();

-- Function to update tag usage counts
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_tag_usage_count()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    IF TG_OP = 'INSERT' THEN
        UPDATE tags 
        SET usage_count = usage_count + 1 
        WHERE tag_id = NEW.tag_id;
    ELSIF TG_OP = 'DELETE' THEN
        UPDATE tags 
        SET usage_count = usage_count - 1 
        WHERE tag_id = OLD.tag_id;
    END IF;
    RETURN NULL;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Trigger for tag usage counts
CREATE TRIGGER update_tag_counts
    AFTER INSERT OR DELETE ON content_tags
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_tag_usage_count();
```

## 3. Estratégia de Indexação Otimizada

**database/schema/v2_indexes_optimization.sql**

```sql
-- ============================================
-- STRATEGIC INDEXING FOR PERFORMANCE
-- ============================================

-- USERS TABLE INDEXES
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_account_status ON users(account_status) WHERE account_status != 'active';
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_date ON users(created_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_last_login ON users(last_login_at DESC) WHERE last_login_at IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_users_deleted ON users(deleted_at) WHERE deleted_at IS NOT NULL;

-- Partial index for active users (most common query)
CREATE INDEX idx_users_active ON users(user_id) 
    WHERE account_status = 'active' AND deleted_at IS NULL;

-- CONTENT TABLE INDEXES
CREATE INDEX idx_content_user ON content(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_content_status ON content(status) WHERE status = 'published';
CREATE INDEX idx_content_type ON content(content_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_content_created_date ON content(created_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_content_published_date ON content(published_date) WHERE published_at IS NOT NULL;
CREATE INDEX idx_content_parent ON content(parent_content_id) WHERE parent

## 1. Dockerfiles

### 1.1 Dockerfile da Aplicação Principal (`docker/app/Dockerfile`)

```dockerfile
# DIYAPP V10 - Application Dockerfile
# Multi-stage build para otimização

# Stage 1: Builder
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de build
RUN apk add --no-cache python3 make g++ git

# Copia arquivos de dependências
COPY package*.json ./
COPY yarn.lock ./

# Instala dependências
RUN yarn install --frozen-lockfile --production=false

# Copia código fonte
COPY . .

# Build da aplicação
RUN yarn build

# Stage 2: Production
FROM node:18-alpine AS production

WORKDIR /app

# Instala apenas runtime necessário
RUN apk add --no-cache curl tzdata

# Cria usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001 -G nodejs

# Copia node_modules e build do stage anterior
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/package.json ./

# Configura timezone
ENV TZ=America/Sao_Paulo

# Variáveis de ambiente
ENV NODE_ENV=production
ENV PORT=3000

# Porta exposta
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Troca para usuário não-root
USER nodejs

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]
```

### 1.2 Dockerfile do Nginx (`docker/nginx/Dockerfile`)

```dockerfile
# DIYAPP V10 - Nginx Dockerfile
FROM nginx:1.24-alpine

# Remove configuração padrão
RUN rm /etc/nginx/conf.d/default.conf

# Copia configuração customizada
COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf
COPY conf.d/ /etc/nginx/conf.d/

# Cria diretório para logs
RUN mkdir -p /var/log/nginx && \
    chown -R nginx:nginx /var/log/nginx

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:80/health || exit 1

EXPOSE 80 443

USER nginx

CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]
```

### 1.3 Dockerfile do PostgreSQL (`docker/postgres/Dockerfile`)

```dockerfile
# DIYAPP V10 - PostgreSQL Dockerfile
FROM postgres:15-alpine

# Instala ferramentas adicionais
RUN apk add --no-cache tzdata

# Copia scripts de inicialização
COPY init-scripts/ /docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/

# Configura timezone
ENV TZ=America/Sao_Paulo

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD pg_isready -U $POSTGRES_USER || exit 1

EXPOSE 5432
```

## 2. Configuração Nginx (`docker/nginx/nginx.conf`)

```nginx
# DIYAPP V10 - Nginx Configuration
user nginx;
worker_processes auto;
error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log warn;
pid /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections 1024;
    use epoll;
    multi_accept on;
}

http {
    include /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type application/octet-stream;

    # Log format
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for" '
                    'rt=$request_time uct="$upstream_connect_time" '
                    'uht="$upstream_header_time" urt="$upstream_response_time"';

    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;

    # Basic Settings
    sendfile on;
    tcp_nopush on;
    tcp_nodelay on;
    keepalive_timeout 65;
    types_hash_max_size 2048;
    server_tokens off;

    # Gzip Settings
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_proxied any;
    gzip_comp_level 6;
    gzip_types
        text/plain
        text/css
        text/xml
        text/javascript
        application/json
        application/javascript
        application/xml+rss
        application/atom+xml
        image/svg+xml;

    # Rate limiting
    limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=api:10m rate=10r/s;
    limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=auth:10m rate=5r/s;

    # Include virtual hosts
    include /etc/nginx/conf.d/*.conf;
}
```

## 3. Docker Compose para Desenvolvimento

### 3.1 `docker-compose.yml` (Desenvolvimento)

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de dados
  postgres:
    build:
      context: ./docker/postgres
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_dev
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-dev_password}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./docker/postgres/init-scripts:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s

  # Aplicação principal
  app:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: ./docker/app/Dockerfile
      target: builder  # Usa stage de build para desenvolvimento
    container_name: diyapp-app
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp_user:${DB_PASSWORD:-dev_password}@postgres:5432/diyapp_dev
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      PORT: 3000
    volumes:
      - .:/app
      - /app/node_modules
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    command: yarn dev
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s

  # Redis para cache e sessões
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-redis_pass}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Nginx como reverse proxy
  nginx:
    build:
      context: ./docker/nginx
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
      - ./logs/nginx:/var/log/nginx
    depends_on:
      - app
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  # Prometheus para monitoramento
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Grafana para dashboards
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin}
      - GF_USERS_ALLOW_SIGN_UP=false
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    name: diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  prometheus_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local
```

### 3.2 `docker-compose.prod.yml` (Produção)

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    extends:
      file: docker-compose.yml
      service: postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_prod
      POSTGRES_USER: ${DB_USER}
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 2G
        reservations:
          memory: 1G
      restart_policy:
        condition: on-failure
        max_attempts: 3
    volumes:
      - /data/postgres:/var/lib/postgresql/data

  app:
    extends:
      file: docker-compose.yml
      service: app
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://${DB_USER}:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp_prod
      REDIS_URL: redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379
    deploy:
      replicas: 3
      update_config:
        parallelism: 1
        delay: 10s
        order: start-first
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 1G
        reservations:
          memory: 512M
      restart_policy:
        condition: on-failure
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s

  nginx:
    extends:
      file: docker-compose.yml
      service: nginx
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 512M
        reservations:
          memory: 256M
      restart_policy:
        condition: on-failure
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"

  redis:
    extends:
      file: docker-compose.yml
      service: redis
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 1G
        reservations:
          memory: 512M
```
