### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Agent Runtime Environment

Vou configurar um ambiente de execução robusto para agentes de IA com interface padrão, gerenciamento de contextos e integração com múltiplos provedores de LLM.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
src/
├── agents/
│   ├── runtime/
│   │   ├── AgentRuntime.js
│   │   ├── ContextManager.js
│   │   └── ProviderRegistry.js
│   ├── providers/
│   │   ├── OpenAIProvider.js
│   │   ├── AnthropicProvider.js
│   │   ├── LocalProvider.js
│   │   └── BaseProvider.js
│   └── core/
│       ├── Agent.js
│       ├── Message.js
│       └── Tool.js
├── observability/
│   ├── LLMObserver.js
│   ├── CostTracker.js
│   └── QualityMonitor.js
├── storage/
│   ├── ContextStore.js
│   └── AgentRegistry.js
├── utils/
│   ├── logger.js
│   └── validation.js
└── api/
    ├── agents.js
    └── contexts.js
public/
├── index.html
├── dashboard.js
└── styles.css
config/
├── providers.json
└── agents.json
```

## Código Principal

### 1. Interface Principal - AgentRuntime.js

```javascript
// src/agents/runtime/AgentRuntime.js
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const ProviderRegistry = require('./ProviderRegistry');
const ContextManager = require('./ContextManager');
const LLMObserver = require('../../observability/LLMObserver');

class AgentRuntime extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(config = {}) {
    super();
    this.config = {
      maxContextLength: 10000,
      defaultProvider: 'openai',
      enableObservability: true,
      ...config
    };
    
    this.providerRegistry = new ProviderRegistry();
    this.contextManager = new ContextManager();
    this.observability = this.config.enableObservability ? new LLMObserver() : null;
    this.activeAgents = new Map();
    this.initialized = false;
    
    this.setupEventHandlers();
  }

  async initialize() {
    try {
      logger.info('Initializing Agent Runtime...');
      
      // Load providers from config
      await this.providerRegistry.loadProviders(this.config.providers);
      
      // Initialize context manager
      await this.contextManager.initialize();
      
      // Setup observability
      if (this.observability) {
        await this.observability.initialize();
      }
      
      this.initialized = true;
      logger.info('Agent Runtime initialized successfully');
      this.emit('initialized');
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to initialize Agent Runtime:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  setupEventHandlers() {
    this.on('agent_created', (agentId) => {
      logger.info(`Agent created: ${agentId}`);
    });

    this.on('agent_destroyed', (agentId) => {
      logger.info(`Agent destroyed: ${agentId}`);
    });

    this.on('llm_call_start', (data) => {
      logger.debug(`LLM call started: ${data.provider}:${data.model}`);
    });

    this.on('llm_call_complete', (data) => {
      logger.debug(`LLM call completed: ${data.provider}:${data.model} - ${data.duration}ms`);
    });

    this.on('context_updated', (agentId, contextSize) => {
      logger.debug(`Context updated for ${agentId}: ${contextSize} tokens`);
    });
  }

  async createAgent(agentConfig) {
    if (!this.initialized) {
      throw new Error('Agent Runtime not initialized');
    }

    const agentId = `agent_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
    
    const agent = {
      id: agentId,
      config: agentConfig,
      context: await this.contextManager.createContext(agentId),
      provider: this.providerRegistry.getProvider(agentConfig.provider || this.config.defaultProvider),
      tools: new Map(),
      state: 'idle',
      createdAt: new Date(),
      lastActive: new Date()
    };

    // Register tools if provided
    if (agentConfig.tools) {
      for (const tool of agentConfig.tools) {
        agent.tools.set(tool.name, tool);
      }
    }

    this.activeAgents.set(agentId, agent);
    this.emit('agent_created', agentId);
    
    return agentId;
  }

  async execute(agentId, input, options = {}) {
    if (!this.activeAgents.has(agentId)) {
      throw new Error(`Agent ${agentId} not found`);
    }

    const agent = this.activeAgents.get(agentId);
    agent.state = 'processing';
    agent.lastActive = new Date();

    try {
      // Update context
      await this.contextManager.addToContext(agentId, {
        role: 'user',
        content: input,
        timestamp: new Date()
      });

      // Prepare messages from context
      const messages = await this.contextManager.getMessages(agentId);
      
      // Execute tool calls if any
      const toolResults = await this.executeTools(agent, input, options);
      
      // Prepare LLM call
      const llmOptions = {
        messages: [...messages, ...toolResults],
        model: agent.config.model || 'gpt-4',
        temperature: agent.config.temperature || 0.7,
        maxTokens: agent.config.maxTokens || 1000,
        ...options
      };

      // Track LLM call
      const callId = this.observability?.startCall({
        agentId,
        provider: agent.provider.name,
        model: llmOptions.model,
        inputTokens: this.estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(llmOptions.messages))
      });

      this.emit('llm_call_start', {
        agentId,
        provider: agent.provider.name,
        model: llmOptions.model
      });

      // Execute LLM call
      const startTime = Date.now();
      const response = await agent.provider.complete(llmOptions);
      const duration = Date.now() - startTime;

      // Update context with response
      await this.contextManager.addToContext(agentId, {
        role: 'assistant',
        content: response.content,
        timestamp: new Date()
      });

      // Track completion
      if (this.observability && callId) {
        this.observability.endCall(callId, {
          success: true,
          outputTokens: this.estimateTokens(response.content),
          duration,
          cost: response.cost || 0
        });
      }

      this.emit('llm_call_complete', {
        agentId,
        provider: agent.provider.name,
        model: llmOptions.model,
        duration,
        tokens: response.usage?.totalTokens || 0
      });

      agent.state = 'idle';
      
      return {
        success: true,
        content: response.content,
        usage: response.usage,
        cost: response.cost,
        duration
      };

    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Error executing agent ${agentId}:`, error);
      
      if (this.observability) {
        this.observability.recordError({
          agentId,
          provider: agent.provider.name,
          error: error.message,
          timestamp: new Date()
        });
      }

      agent.state = 'error';
      
      // Fallback logic
      if (options.fallbackProvider) {
        logger.warn(`Attempting fallback to ${options.fallbackProvider}`);
        agent.provider = this.providerRegistry.getProvider(options.fallbackProvider);
        return this.execute(agentId, input, { ...options, fallbackProvider: null });
      }

      throw error;
    }
  }

  async executeTools(agent, input, options) {
    const toolResults = [];
    
    // Check for tool calls in input
    const toolCalls = this.detectToolCalls(input);
    
    for (const toolCall of toolCalls) {
      if (agent.tools.has(toolCall.name)) {
        const tool = agent.tools.get(toolCall.name);
        
        try {
          const result = await tool.execute(toolCall.arguments, {
            agentId: agent.id,
            context: agent.context
          });
          
          toolResults.push({
            role: 'tool',
            name: toolCall.name,
            content: JSON.stringify(result)
          });
          
        } catch (error) {
          logger.error(`Tool execution failed: ${toolCall.name}`, error);
          toolResults.push({
            role: 'tool',
            name: toolCall.name,
            content: `Error: ${error.message}`
          });
        }
      }
    }
    
    return toolResults;
  }

  detectToolCalls(input) {
    // Simple pattern matching for tool calls
    // In production, this would use proper parsing
    const toolCallPattern = /@(\w+)\((.*?)\)/g;
    const calls = [];
    let match;
    
    while ((match = toolCallPattern.exec(input)) !== null) {
      calls.push({
        name: match[1],
        arguments: this.parseArguments(match[2])
      });
    }
    
    return calls;
  }

  parseArguments(argString) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(`{${argString}}`);
    } catch {
      // Simple key-value parsing
      const args = {};
      argString.split(',').forEach(pair => {
        const [key, value] = pair.split('=');
        if (key && value) {
          args[key.trim()] = value.trim();
        }
      });
      return args;
    }
  }

  estimateTokens(text) {
    // Simple estimation: 1 token ≈ 4 characters for English
    return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
  }

  async destroyAgent(agentId) {
    if (this.activeAgents.has(agentId)) {
      const agent = this.activeAgents.get(agentId);
      
      // Save context before destroying
      await this.contextManager.persistContext(agentId);
      
      this.activeAgents.delete(agentId);
      this.emit('agent_destroyed', agentId);
      
      logger.info(`Agent destroyed: ${agentId}`);
      return true;
    }
    
    return false;
  }

  getAgentStatus(agentId) {
    const agent = this.activeAgents.get(agentId);
    if (!agent) return null;
    
    return {
      id: agent.id,
      state: agent.state,
      provider: agent.provider.name,
      contextSize: agent.context?.length || 0,
      createdAt: agent.createdAt,
      lastActive: agent.lastActive,
      tools: Array.from(agent.tools.keys())
    };
  }

  getAllAgents() {
    return Array.from(this.activeAgents.keys()).map(id => this.getAgentStatus(id));
  }

  async shutdown() {
    logger.info('Shutting down Agent Runtime...');
    
    // Persist all contexts
    for (const [agentId] of this.activeAgents) {
      await this.contextManager.persistContext(agentId);
    }
    
    // Clear active agents
    this.activeAgents.clear();
    
    // Shutdown observability
    if (this.observability) {
      await this.observability.shutdown();
    }
    
    this.initialized = false;
    logger.info('Agent Runtime shutdown complete');
  }
}

module.exports = AgentRuntime;
```

### 2. Gerenciador de Contextos - ContextManager.js

```javascript
// src/agents/runtime/ContextManager.js
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const ContextStore = require('../../storage/ContextStore');

class ContextManager {
  constructor(config = {}) {
    this.config = {
      maxContextLength: 10000,
      persistenceInterval: 60000, // 1 minute
      ...config
    };
    
    this.store = new ContextStore();
    this.contexts = new Map();
    this.persistenceTimer = null;
  }

  async initialize() {
    await this.store.initialize();
    this.startPersistenceTimer();
    logger.info('Context Manager initialized');
  }

  startPersistenceTimer() {
    this.persistenceTimer = setInterval(() => {
      this.persistAllContexts().catch(error => {
        logger.error('Error in context persistence:', error);
      });
    }, this.config.persistenceInterval);
  }

  async createContext(agentId, initialMessages = []) {
    const context = {
      id: agentId,
      messages: [...initialMessages],
      metadata: {
        created: new Date(),
        lastUpdated: new Date(),
        version: 1
      }
    };
    
    this.contexts.set(agentId, context);
    await this.store.saveContext(agentId, context);
    
    logger.debug(`Context created for agent: ${agentId}`);
    return context;
  }

  async getContext(agentId) {
    if (this.contexts.has(agentId)) {
      return this.contexts.get(agentId);
    }
    
    // Try to load from store
    const context = await this.store.loadContext(agentId);
    if (context) {
      this.contexts.set(agentId, context);
      return context;
    }
    
    return null;
  }

  async addToContext(agentId, message) {
    const context = await this.getContext(agentId);
    if (!context) {
      throw new Error(`Context not found for agent: ${agentId}`);
    }

    context.messages.push(message);
    context.metadata.lastUpdated = new Date();
    context.metadata.version++;

    // Trim context if too large
    if (this.estimateTokens(JSON.stringify(context.messages)) > this.config.maxContextLength) {
      this.trimContext(context);
    }

    this.contexts.set(agentId, context);
    
    // Emit event for observability
    if (this.runtime) {
      this.runtime.emit('context_updated', agentId, context.messages.length);
    }
    
    return context;
  }

  async getMessages(agentId, limit = null) {
    const context = await this.getContext(agentId);
    if (!context) return [];
    
    const messages = context.messages.map(msg => ({
      role: msg.role,
      content: msg.content
    }));
    
    return limit ? messages.slice(-limit) : messages;
  }

  async clearContext(agentId) {
    const context = await this.getContext(agentId);
    if (context) {
      context.messages = [];
      context.metadata.lastUpdated = new Date();
      context.metadata.version++;
      
      this.contexts.set(agentId, context);
      await this.store.saveContext(agentId, context);
      
      logger.debug(`Context cleared for agent: ${agentId}`);
    }
  }

  trimContext(context) {
    // Remove oldest messages while keeping system messages
    const systemMessages = context.messages.filter(msg => msg.role === 'system');
    const otherMessages = context.messages.filter(msg => msg.role !== 'system');
    
    // Keep all system messages and recent other messages
    const maxOtherMessages = Math.max(10, Math.floor(this.config.maxContextLength * 0.7));
    const trimmedMessages = [
      ...systemMessages,
      ...otherMessages.slice(-maxOtherMessages)
    ];
    
    context.messages = trimmedMessages;
  }

  estimateTokens(text) {
    return Math.ceil(text.length / 4);
  }

  async persistContext(agentId) {
    const context = this.contexts.get(agentId);
    if (context) {
      await this.store.saveContext(agentId, context);
      logger.debug(`Context persisted for agent: ${agentId}`);
    }
  }

  async persistAllContexts() {
    const promises = Array.from(this.contexts.keys()).map(agentId =>
      this.persistContext(agentId)
    );
    
    await Promise.all(promises);
    logger.debug('All contexts persisted');
  }

  async deleteContext(agentId) {
    this.contexts.delete(agentId);
    await this.store.deleteContext(agentId);
    logger.debug(`Context deleted for agent: ${agentId}`);
  }

  setRuntime(runtime) {
    this.runtime = runtime;
  }

  async shutdown() {
    if (this.persistenceTimer) {
      clearInterval(this.persistenceTimer);
    }
    
    await this.persistAllContexts();
    logger.info('Context Manager shutdown complete');
  }
}

module.exports = ContextManager;
```

### 3. Registry de Provedores - ProviderRegistry.js

```javascript
// src/agents/runtime/ProviderRegistry.js
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const OpenAIProvider = require('../providers/OpenAIProvider');
const AnthropicProvider = require('../providers/AnthropicProvider');
const LocalProvider = require('../providers/LocalProvider');

class ProviderRegistry {
  constructor() {
    this.providers = new Map();
    this.defaultProvider = null;
  }

  async loadProviders(config = {}) {
    logger.info('Loading LLM providers...');
    
    // Load from config or use defaults
    const providerConfigs = config.providers || {
      openai: {
        apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY,
        defaultModel: 'gpt-4',
        enabled: true
      },
      anthropic: {
        apiKey: process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY,
        defaultModel: 'claude-3-opus-20240229',
        enabled: true
      },
      local: {
        endpoint: process.env.LOCAL_LLM_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:11434',
        defaultModel: 'llama2',
        enabled: false
      }
    };

    // Initialize providers
    for (const [name, providerConfig] of Object.entries(providerConfigs)) {
      if (providerConfig.enabled) {
        await this.registerProvider(name, providerConfig);
      }
    }

    // Set default provider
    this.defaultProvider = config.defaultProvider || 'openai';
    
    logger.info(`Providers loaded: ${Array.from(this.providers.keys()).join(', ')}`);
  }

  async registerProvider(name, config) {
    let provider;
    
    switch (name.toLowerCase()) {
      case 'openai':
        provider = new OpenAIProvider(config);
        break;
      case 'anthropic':
        provider = new AnthropicProvider(config);
        break;
      case 'local':
        provider = new LocalProvider(config);
        break;
      default:
        throw new Error(`Unknown provider: ${name}`);
    }
    
    await provider.initialize();
    this.providers.set(name, provider);
    
    logger.info(`Provider registered: ${name}`);

## 2. Threat Modeling - Análise STRIDE

```python
# security/threat_modeling/stride_analysis.py
"""
Threat Modeling Analysis for DIYAPP V10 Core Architecture
Using STRIDE Framework
"""

from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
from datetime import datetime
import json

class ThreatCategory(Enum):
    SPOOFING = "Spoofing"
    TAMPERING = "Tampering"
    REPUDIATION = "Repudiation"
    INFORMATION_DISCLOSURE = "Information Disclosure"
    DENIAL_OF_SERVICE = "Denial of Service"
    ELEVATION_OF_PRIVILEGE = "Elevation of Privilege"

class RiskLevel(Enum):
    CRITICAL = "Critical"
    HIGH = "High"
    MEDIUM = "Medium"
    LOW = "Low"

@dataclass
class Threat:
    id: str
    category: ThreatCategory
    description: str
    attack_vector: str
    impact: str
    risk_level: RiskLevel
    mitigation: List[str]
    affected_components: List[str]
    cvss_score: Optional[float] = None
    
class STRIDEAnalyzer:
    def __init__(self, architecture: Dict):
        self.architecture = architecture
        self.threats = []
        self._initialize_threats()
    
    def _initialize_threats(self):
        """Initialize common threats for web applications"""
        
        # Spoofing Threats
        self.threats.extend([
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-S-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.SPOOFING,
                description="Authentication token theft or forgery",
                attack_vector="Steal JWT via XSS or MITM",
                impact="Impersonation of legitimate users",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Use HttpOnly, Secure cookies for tokens",
                    "Implement short-lived access tokens (15min)",
                    "Use refresh tokens with device binding",
                    "Implement token binding",
                    "Enable MFA for sensitive operations"
                ],
                affected_components=["Auth Service", "API Gateway", "Frontend"],
                cvss_score=8.2
            ),
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-S-002",
                category=ThreatCategory.SPOOFING,
                description="Credential stuffing attacks",
                attack_vector="Automated login attempts with breached credentials",
                impact="Account takeover",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Implement rate limiting on auth endpoints",
                    "Require MFA for unrecognized devices",
                    "Monitor for credential stuffing patterns",
                    "Use CAPTCHA after failed attempts"
                ],
                affected_components=["Auth Service", "Login API"],
                cvss_score=7.4
            )
        ])
        
        # Tampering Threats
        self.threats.extend([
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-T-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.TAMPERING,
                description="SQL Injection",
                attack_vector="Malicious SQL in user inputs",
                impact="Data manipulation, extraction, or deletion",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.CRITICAL,
                mitigation=[
                    "Use parameterized queries exclusively",
                    "Implement ORM with built-in protection",
                    "Regular SQLi scanning",
                    "Input validation with strict schemas"
                ],
                affected_components=["Database Layer", "API Endpoints"],
                cvss_score=9.8
            ),
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-T-002",
                category=ThreatCategory.TAMPERING,
                description="Cross-Site Request Forgery (CSRF)",
                attack_vector="Forge requests from authenticated sessions",
                impact="Unauthorized actions on behalf of user",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Implement CSRF tokens",
                    "Use SameSite cookies (Strict)",
                    "Check Origin/Referer headers",
                    "Require re-authentication for sensitive actions"
                ],
                affected_components=["Frontend", "API Endpoints"],
                cvss_score=8.1
            )
        ])
        
        # Information Disclosure Threats
        self.threats.extend([
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-I-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.INFORMATION_DISCLOSURE,
                description="Sensitive data exposure in logs",
                attack_vector="Access to application logs",
                impact="PII, credentials, or tokens exposed",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Implement data masking in logs",
                    "Use structured logging with redaction",
                    "Encrypt log files at rest",
                    "Restrict log access with RBAC"
                ],
                affected_components=["Logging System", "Monitoring"],
                cvss_score=7.5
            ),
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-I-002",
                category=ThreatCategory.INFORMATION_DISCLOSURE,
                description="Insecure Direct Object References (IDOR)",
                attack_vector="Manipulate object IDs in requests",
                impact="Unauthorized access to other users' data",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Implement access control checks per resource",
                    "Use UUIDs instead of sequential IDs",
                    "Validate ownership before operations",
                    "Implement resource-level authorization"
                ],
                affected_components=["API Endpoints", "Business Logic"],
                cvss_score=8.2
            )
        ])
        
        # Denial of Service Threats
        self.threats.extend([
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-D-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.DENIAL_OF_SERVICE,
                description="API Rate Limiting Bypass",
                attack_vector="Distributed requests from multiple IPs",
                impact="Service degradation or unavailability",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                mitigation=[
                    "Implement distributed rate limiting",
                    "Use API Gateway with WAF",
                    "Implement circuit breakers",
                    "Monitor for abnormal traffic patterns"
                ],
                affected_components=["API Gateway", "Load Balancer"],
                cvss_score=7.5
            )
        ])
        
        # Elevation of Privilege Threats
        self.threats.extend([
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-E-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.ELEVATION_OF_PRIVILEGE,
                description="JWT Token Manipulation",
                attack_vector="Modify JWT claims to gain admin access",
                impact="Privilege escalation to admin level",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.CRITICAL,
                mitigation=[
                    "Sign tokens with strong asymmetric keys (RS256)",
                    "Validate token signatures strictly",
                    "Implement token revocation mechanism",
                    "Use short token expiration"
                ],
                affected_components=["Auth Service", "API Middleware"],
                cvss_score=9.1
            )
        ])
    
    def generate_report(self) -> Dict:
        """Generate comprehensive threat modeling report"""
        report = {
            "metadata": {
                "project": "DIYAPP V10 Core",
                "version": "1.0.0",
                "date": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                "framework": "STRIDE"
            },
            "summary": {
                "total_threats": len(self.threats),
                "by_category": self._count_by_category(),
                "by_risk": self._count_by_risk()
            },
            "threats": [self._threat_to_dict(t) for t in self.threats],
            "recommendations": self._generate_recommendations()
        }
        return report
    
    def _count_by_category(self) -> Dict:
        counts = {cat.value: 0 for cat in ThreatCategory}
        for threat in self.threats:
            counts[threat.category.value] += 1
        return counts
    
    def _count_by_risk(self) -> Dict:
        counts = {risk.value: 0 for risk in RiskLevel}
        for threat in self.threats:
            counts[threat.risk_level.value] += 1
        return counts
    
    def _threat_to_dict(self, threat: Threat) -> Dict:
        return {
            "id": threat.id,
            "category": threat.category.value,
            "description": threat.description,
            "attack_vector": threat.attack_vector,
            "impact": threat.impact,
            "risk_level": threat.risk_level.value,
            "cvss_score": threat.cvss_score,
            "mitigation": threat.mitigation,
            "affected_components": threat.affected_components
        }
    
    def _generate_recommendations(self) -> List[str]:
        return [
            "Implement all critical mitigations before production deployment",
            "Conduct regular security training for developers",
            "Establish bug bounty program",
            "Implement automated security testing in CI/CD",
            "Regularly update threat model with architecture changes"
        ]

# Example usage
if __name__ == "__main__":
    architecture = {
        "components": ["Frontend", "API Gateway", "Auth Service", "Database"],
        "technologies": ["React", "Node.js", "PostgreSQL", "Redis"],
        "data_flows": ["User -> Frontend -> API -> Services"]
    }
    
    analyzer = STRIDEAnalyzer(architecture)
    report = analyzer.generate_report()
    
    with open("threat_model_report.json", "w") as f:
        json.dump(report, f, indent=2)
    
    print("Threat modeling report generated: threat_model_report.json")
```

## 3. Política de Autenticação e Autorização

```python
# security/auth/auth_policy.py
"""
Authentication and Authorization Policy for DIYAPP V10
JWT-based authentication with RBAC/ABAC
"""

import os
import time
import json
import hashlib
import secrets
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Tuple
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum
import jwt
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import redis
from pydantic import BaseModel, validator, Field
import bcrypt

# Configuration
class AuthConfig:
    # JWT Configuration
    JWT_ALGORITHM = "RS256"  # Asymmetric for better security
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES = 15
    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS = 7
    MFA_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES = 5
    
    # Password Policy
    MIN_PASSWORD_LENGTH = 12
    REQUIRE_COMPLEXITY = True
    PASSWORD_HISTORY_SIZE = 5
    MAX_FAILED_ATTEMPTS = 5
    LOCKOUT_DURATION_MINUTES = 15
    
    # Session Management
    MAX_CONCURRENT_SESSIONS = 5
    SESSION_INACTIVITY_TIMEOUT = 30  # minutes

# Data Models
class UserRole(str, Enum):
    GUEST = "guest"
    USER = "user"
    EDITOR = "editor"
    ADMIN = "admin"
    SUPER_ADMIN = "super_admin"

class Permission(str, Enum):
    # Resource-based permissions
    USER_READ = "user:read"
    USER_WRITE = "user:write"
    USER_DELETE = "user:delete"
    
    CONTENT_READ = "content:read"
    CONTENT_WRITE = "content:write"
    CONTENT_DELETE = "content:delete"
    
    ADMIN_READ = "admin:read"
    ADMIN_WRITE = "admin:write"
    ADMIN_DELETE = "admin:delete"
    
    SYSTEM_MANAGE = "system:manage"

@dataclass
class UserSession:
    session_id: str
    user_id: str
    device_fingerprint: str
    ip_address: str
    user_agent: str
    created_at: datetime
    last_activity: datetime
    is_active: bool
    mfa_verified: bool = False

@dataclass
class JWTClaims:
    """Standard JWT claims with custom extensions"""
    # Standard claims
    sub: str  # Subject (user ID)
    exp: int  # Expiration time
    iat: int  # Issued at
    jti: str  # JWT ID
    
    # Custom claims
    roles: List[UserRole]
    permissions: List[Permission]
    session_id: str
    device_id: str
    mfa_verified: bool
    
    @classmethod
    def create(cls, user_id: str, roles: List[UserRole], 
               permissions: List[Permission], session_id: str, 
               device_id: str, mfa_verified: bool = False) -> 'JWTClaims':
        now = int(time.time())
        return cls(
            sub=user_id,
            exp=now + (AuthConfig.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60),
            iat=now,
            jti=secrets.token_urlsafe(32),
            roles=roles,
            permissions=permissions,
            session_id=session_id,
            device_id=device_id,
            mfa_verified=mfa_verified
        )

# RBAC Configuration
class RBACPolicy:
    """Role-Based Access Control Policy"""
    
    ROLE_PERMISSIONS = {
        UserRole.GUEST: [
            Permission.CONTENT_READ
        ],
        UserRole.USER: [
            Permission.USER_READ,
            Permission.USER_WRITE,
            Permission.CONTENT_READ,
            Permission.CONTENT_WRITE
        ],
        UserRole.EDITOR: [
            Permission.USER_READ,
            Permission.CONTENT_READ,
            Permission.CONTENT_WRITE,
            Permission.CONTENT_DELETE
        ],
        UserRole.ADMIN: [
            Permission.USER_READ,
            Permission.USER_WRITE,
            Permission.USER_DELETE,
            Permission.CONTENT_READ,
            Permission.CONTENT_WRITE,
            Permission.CONTENT_DELETE,
            Permission.ADMIN_READ,
            Permission.ADMIN_WRITE
        ],
        UserRole.SUPER_ADMIN: [
            Permission.SYSTEM_MANAGE,
            *list(Permission)  # All permissions
        ]
    }
    
    @classmethod
    def get_permissions_for_role(cls, role: UserRole) -> List[Permission]:
        return cls.ROLE_PERMISSIONS.get(role, [])
    
    @classmethod
    def has_permission(cls, role: UserRole, permission: Permission) -> bool:
        return permission in cls.ROLE_PERMISSIONS.get(role, [])

# Authentication Service
class AuthenticationService:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path: str, public_key_path: str):
        self.private_key = self._load_private_key(private_key_path)
        self.public_key = self._load_public_key(public_key_path)
        self.redis_client = redis.Redis(
            host=os.getenv('REDIS_HOST', 'localhost'),
            port=int(os.getenv('REDIS_PORT', 6379)),
            db=0,
            decode_responses=True
        )
        
    def _load_private_key(self, path: str) -> str:
        """Load RSA private key from file"""
        with open(path, 'r') as f:
            return f.read()
    
    def _load_public_key(self, path: str) -> str:
        """Load RSA public key from file"""
        with open(path, 'r') as f:
            return f.read()
    
    def hash_password(self, password: str) -> str:
        """Hash password with bcrypt"""
        salt = bcrypt.gensalt(rounds=12)
        hashed = bcrypt.hashpw(password.encode('utf-8'), salt)
        return hashed.decode('utf-8')
    
    def verify_password(self, password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
        """Verify password against hash"""
        return bcrypt.checkpw(
            password.encode('utf-8'),
            hashed_password.encode('utf-8')
        )
    
    def create_session(self, user_id: str, device_info: Dict[str, str]) -> UserSession:
        """Create new user session"""
        session_id = secrets.token_urlsafe(32)
        device_fingerprint = self._generate_device_fingerprint(device_info)
        
        session = UserSession(
            session_id=session_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            device_fingerprint=device_fingerprint,
            ip_address=device_info.get('ip', ''),
            user_agent=device_info.get('user_agent', ''),
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            last_activity=datetime.now(),
            is_active=True
        )
        
        # Store session in Redis
        session_key = f"session:{session_id}"
        self.redis_client.hset(session_key, mapping=asdict(session))
        self.redis_client.expire(
            session_key, 
            AuthConfig.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS * 24 * 3600
        )
        
        # Track user sessions
        user_sessions_key = f"user_sessions:{user_id}"
        self.redis_client.sadd(user_sessions_key, session_id)
        
        return session
    
    def _generate_device_fingerprint(self, device_info: Dict) -> str:
        """Generate unique device fingerprint"""
        fingerprint_data = json.dumps(device_info, sort_keys=True)

## 1. Modelo de Dados com Compliance LGPD/GDPR

**src/models/data_schema.js**
```javascript
/**
 * Modelo de Dados V10 com Compliance LGPD/GDPR
 * Classificação de dados pessoais e políticas de retenção
 */

const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');

class DataSchema {
  constructor(sequelize) {
    this.sequelize = sequelize;
    this.models = {};
    this.initModels();
  }

  initModels() {
    // 1. Tabela de Usuários (Titulares de Dados)
    this.models.User = this.sequelize.define('User', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      email: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false,
        unique: true,
        comment: 'Dado pessoal - necessário para autenticação'
      },
      phone: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        comment: 'Dado pessoal - opcional para notificações'
      },
      full_name: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        comment: 'Dado pessoal - para personalização'
      },
      consent_given_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        comment: 'Data do consentimento LGPD/GDPR'
      },
      consent_version: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        defaultValue: '1.0'
      },
      legal_basis: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('consent', 'contract', 'legal_obligation', 'legitimate_interest'),
        defaultValue: 'consent'
      },
      data_retention_category: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('conversation_data', 'account_data', 'payment_data', 'audit_log'),
        defaultValue: 'account_data'
      },
      retention_period_days: {
        type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
        defaultValue: 730, // 2 anos padrão para dados de conta
        comment: 'Período de retenção específico para este usuário'
      },
      deletion_scheduled_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        comment: 'Data programada para exclusão automática'
      },
      gdpr_applies: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false,
        comment: 'GDPR aplicável para usuários da UE'
      },
      country: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING(2),
        comment: 'Código do país para determinação de jurisdição'
      }
    }, {
      tableName: 'users',
      timestamps: true,
      paranoid: true, // Soft delete para rastreamento de exclusões
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['deletion_scheduled_at'] },
        { fields: ['data_retention_category'] },
        { fields: ['gdpr_applies'] }
      ]
    });

    // 2. Tabela de Conversas
    this.models.Conversation = this.sequelize.define('Conversation', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      user_id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: false,
        references: {
          model: 'users',
          key: 'id'
        }
      },
      session_id: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        unique: true
      },
      platform: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('whatsapp', 'web', 'api', 'telegram'),
        defaultValue: 'web'
      },
      conversation_data: {
        type: DataTypes.JSONB,
        comment: 'Dados da conversa - pode conter dados pessoais'
      },
      contains_personal_data: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false
      },
      data_classification: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('public', 'internal', 'confidential', 'restricted'),
        defaultValue: 'internal'
      },
      retention_period_days: {
        type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
        defaultValue: 180, // 6 meses para logs de conversa
        comment: 'LGPD: período proporcional à finalidade'
      },
      auto_delete_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        comment: 'Data para exclusão automática'
      },
      llm_processed: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        defaultValue: false,
        comment: 'Indica se dados foram enviados para LLM'
      },
      llm_provider: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        comment: 'Provedor do LLM (Anthropic, OpenAI, etc.)'
      }
    }, {
      tableName: 'conversations',
      timestamps: true,
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['user_id'] },
        { fields: ['auto_delete_at'] },
        { fields: ['contains_personal_data'] },
        { fields: ['created_at'] }
      ]
    });

    // 3. Tabela de Logs de Auditoria
    this.models.AuditLog = this.sequelize.define('AuditLog', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      event_type: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM(
          'data_access',
          'data_modification',
          'data_deletion',
          'consent_change',
          'user_request',
          'security_incident',
          'system_action'
        ),
        allowNull: false
      },
      user_id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: true
      },
      ip_address: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING(45),
        comment: 'IPv4 ou IPv6'
      },
      user_agent: {
        type: DataTypes.TEXT
      },
      resource_type: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        comment: 'Tipo de recurso afetado'
      },
      resource_id: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING
      },
      action_details: {
        type: DataTypes.JSONB,
        comment: 'Detalhes específicos da ação'
      },
      compliance_metadata: {
        type: DataTypes.JSONB,
        defaultValue: {},
        comment: 'Metadados para LGPD/GDPR'
      },
      retention_period_days: {
        type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
        defaultValue: 365, // 1 ano para logs de auditoria
        comment: 'ISO 27001: logs devem ser mantidos por período adequado'
      },
      auto_delete_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE
      }
    }, {
      tableName: 'audit_logs',
      timestamps: true,
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['event_type'] },
        { fields: ['user_id'] },
        { fields: ['created_at'] },
        { fields: ['auto_delete_at'] }
      ]
    });

    // 4. Tabela de Solicitações de Titulares
    this.models.DataSubjectRequest = this.sequelize.define('DataSubjectRequest', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      user_id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: false
      },
      request_type: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM(
          'access',
          'correction',
          'deletion',
          'portability',
          'objection',
          'consent_withdrawal'
        ),
        allowNull: false
      },
      request_status: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM(
          'received',
          'in_progress',
          'completed',
          'rejected',
          'cancelled'
        ),
        defaultValue: 'received'
      },
      request_details: {
        type: DataTypes.JSONB,
        comment: 'Detalhes específicos da solicitação'
      },
      deadline_date: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        comment: 'Data limite para resposta (15 dias LGPD)'
      },
      response_data: {
        type: DataTypes.JSONB,
        comment: 'Dados da resposta ao titular'
      },
      verified_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        comment: 'Data da verificação de identidade'
      },
      verification_method: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM('email', 'phone', 'document', 'existing_session'),
        comment: 'Método de verificação de identidade'
      }
    }, {
      tableName: 'data_subject_requests',
      timestamps: true,
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['user_id'] },
        { fields: ['request_type'] },
        { fields: ['request_status'] },
        { fields: ['deadline_date'] }
      ]
    });

    // 5. Tabela de Consentimentos
    this.models.ConsentRecord = this.sequelize.define('ConsentRecord', {
      id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
        primaryKey: true
      },
      user_id: {
        type: DataTypes.UUID,
        allowNull: false
      },
      consent_type: {
        type: DataTypes.ENUM(
          'privacy_policy',
          'terms_of_service',
          'marketing_emails',
          'data_processing',
          'third_party_sharing',
          'cookies'
        ),
        allowNull: false
      },
      consent_given: {
        type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
        allowNull: false
      },
      consent_version: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING,
        allowNull: false
      },
      granted_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE,
        allowNull: false
      },
      revoked_at: {
        type: DataTypes.DATE
      },
      ip_address: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING(45)
      },
      user_agent: {
        type: DataTypes.TEXT
      },
      session_id: {
        type: DataTypes.STRING
      }
    }, {
      tableName: 'consent_records',
      timestamps: true,
      indexes: [
        { fields: ['user_id'] },
        { fields: ['consent_type'] },
        { fields: ['consent_given'] },
        { fields: ['granted_at'] }
      ]
    });

    // Definir relacionamentos
    this.defineRelationships();
  }

  defineRelationships() {
    // Usuário tem muitas conversas
    this.models.User.hasMany(this.models.Conversation, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id',
      onDelete: 'CASCADE'
    });
    this.models.Conversation.belongsTo(this.models.User, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id'
    });

    // Usuário tem muitas solicitações
    this.models.User.hasMany(this.models.DataSubjectRequest, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id',
      onDelete: 'CASCADE'
    });
    this.models.DataSubjectRequest.belongsTo(this.models.User, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id'
    });

    // Usuário tem muitos consentimentos
    this.models.User.hasMany(this.models.ConsentRecord, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id',
      onDelete: 'CASCADE'
    });
    this.models.ConsentRecord.belongsTo(this.models.User, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id'
    });

    // Usuário tem muitos logs de auditoria
    this.models.User.hasMany(this.models.AuditLog, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id',
      onDelete: 'SET NULL'
    });
    this.models.AuditLog.belongsTo(this.models.User, {
      foreignKey: 'user_id'
    });
  }

  async syncModels() {
    await this.sequelize.sync({ alter: true });
    console.log('Modelos de dados sincronizados com compliance LGPD/GDPR');
  }
}

module.exports = DataSchema;
```

## 2. Políticas de Retenção de Dados

**src/compliance/data_retention/retention_policy.js**
```javascript
/**
 * Políticas de Retenção LGPD/GDPR
 * Períodos baseados na finalidade e necessidade
 */

class RetentionPolicy {
  constructor() {
    // Políticas de retenção por categoria de dados
    this.policies = {
      // Dados de Conta do Usuário
      account_data: {
        retention_days: 730, // 2 anos
        legal_basis: 'contract',
        description: 'Dados necessários para prestação do serviço',
        auto_delete: true,
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(b)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, V'
      },

      // Dados de Conversa/Chat
      conversation_data: {
        retention_days: 180, // 6 meses
        legal_basis: 'legitimate_interest',
        description: 'Histórico para melhoria do serviço e suporte',
        auto_delete: true,
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(f)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, IX'
      },

      // Logs de Auditoria
      audit_log: {
        retention_days: 365, // 1 ano
        legal_basis: 'legal_obligation',
        description: 'Requisito de segurança e conformidade',
        auto_delete: true,
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(c)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, II',
        iso_27001: 'A.12.4.1'
      },

      // Dados de Pagamento
      payment_data: {
        retention_days: 1825, // 5 anos
        legal_basis: 'legal_obligation',
        description: 'Requisitos fiscais e contábeis',
        auto_delete: false, // Exclusão manual após revisão
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(c)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, II'
      },

      // Cookies e Rastreamento
      cookie_data: {
        retention_days: 90, // 3 meses
        legal_basis: 'consent',
        description: 'Preferências do usuário e analytics',
        auto_delete: true,
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(a)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, I'
      },

      // Dados para Marketing
      marketing_data: {
        retention_days: 365, // 1 ano
        legal_basis: 'consent',
        description: 'Comunicações de marketing',
        auto_delete: true,
        gdpr_article: '6(1)(a)',
        lgpd_article: '7º, I'
      },

      // Backups do Sistema
      backup_data: {
        retention_days: 30, // 30 dias
        legal_basis: 'legitimate_interest',
        description: 'Recuperação de desastres',
        auto_delete: true,
        encryption_required: true,
        gdpr_article: '32'
      }
    };

    // Regras específicas por jurisdição
    this.jurisdictionRules = {
      BR: { // Brasil - LGPD
        min_retention: {
          fiscal: 1825, // 5 anos para dados fiscais
          labor: 3650   // 10 anos para dados trabalhistas
        },
        authority: 'ANPD',
        notification_period: 72 // horas para notificação de incidentes
      },
      EU: { // União Europeia - GDPR
        min_retention: {
          financial: 1825, // 5 anos para transações financeiras
          medical: 3650    // 10 anos para dados médicos
        },
        authority: 'DPA',
        notification_period: 72 // horas
      },
      US: { // Estados Unidos
        min_retention: {
          hipaa: 3650, // 10 anos para dados de saúde
          pci: 365     // 1 ano para dados de pagamento
        }
      }
    };
  }

  /**
   * Determina política de retenção com base no tipo de dado
   */
  getPolicy(dataCategory, jurisdiction = 'BR') {
    const basePolicy = this.policies[dataCategory];
    if (!basePolicy) {
      throw new Error(`Categoria de dados não encontrada: ${dataCategory}`);
    }

    // Ajustar por jurisdição se necessário
    const jurisdictionRule = this.jurisdictionRules[jurisdiction];
    if (jurisdictionRule && jurisdictionRule.min_retention) {
      // Verificar se há requisito mínimo específico
      for (const [category, minDays] of Object

                        <p><strong>INVALIDADO se:</strong> Acurácia < 70% ou tempo de resposta > 5s</p>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="criterion">
                        <h5>Otimização de Fluxos</h5>
                        <p><strong>VALIDADO se:</strong> Reduz abandonos em 30% em fluxos complexos</p>
                        <p><strong>INVALIDADO se:</strong> Usuários ignoram 80%+ das sugestões</p>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="action-buttons">
                        <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="submitToBacklog()">
                            <i class="fas fa-tasks"></i> Enviar para Backlog PM
                        </button>
                        <button class="btn btn-warning" onclick="scheduleReview()">
                            <i class="fas fa-calendar-alt"></i> Agendar Revisão Técnica
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>
        </div>

        <!-- Radar de Inovação -->
        <section class="card radar-card">
            <h2><i class="fas fa-satellite-dish"></i> Radar de Inovação - IA Generativa</h2>
            <div class="radar-grid">
                <div class="radar-quadrant adopt">
                    <h3>Adotar Agora</h3>

                        <li>GPT-4 para análise de texto</li>

                    </ul>
                </div>
                <div class="radar-quadrant experiment">
                    <h3>Experimentar</h3>

                <div class="radar-quadrant observe">

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10/
├── docker/
│   ├── Dockerfile.api
│   ├── Dockerfile.frontend
│   ├── Dockerfile.worker
│   └── Dockerfile.monitoring
├── docker-compose.yml
├── docker-compose.prod.yml
├── k8s/
│   ├── namespace.yaml
│   ├── configmap.yaml
│   ├── secrets.yaml
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── deployment.yaml
│   │   ├── service.yaml
│   │   └── hpa.yaml
│   ├── frontend/
│   │   ├── deployment.yaml
│   │   └── service.yaml
│   ├── worker/
│   │   ├── deployment.yaml
│   │   └── hpa.yaml
│   ├── monitoring/
│   │   ├── prometheus.yaml
│   │   ├── grafana.yaml
│   │   └── loki.yaml
